In other words, it squares up the image for you.\r\n\r\nSplitting an image up into sections, to help us draw it, is something humans have been doing for centuries. With the dawn of the twenty-first century, though, it seems we have let this technique stagnate. We are still drawing the grid by hand and that includes computers (line or pen tool anyone?). I am sure you agree when I say it is a good thing to teach children how to do by hand in their art class. But... it becomes tedious the more you do it and, once you know how to do it, there is very little to learn or improve upon. This is where Paint Grid comes in.\r\n\r\nTo use Paint Grid, drag and drop a .jpg or .png file into the preview area. Use the control panel on the right to adjust the amount of rows and columns you want. After that, set the thickness of the grid lines and its colour and when you are ready, click \"Save As\". From there, you can either print it or open it in your go-to painting/drawing application.\r\n\r\nBy using Paint Grid, you are reducing a task which can take tens of minutes (sometimes over an hour) to mere seconds. All you changes happen in real-time, as well, so you are no longer bound to a certain size once you start. If you do not like the look of your grid, make a change and watch it update straight away. If you are bad at maths, play about with the settings until you find something you like. Write music, using your digital pen*, and StaffPad will transform your handwritten notation into a beautifully typeset score which you can then edit, play back, print and share. For composers and musicians, StaffPad revolutionises the art of writing music.\r\n\r\n*IMPORTANT NOTE: STAFFPAD **REQUIRES** A DEVICE WITH ACTIVE PEN CAPABILITIES. As you move from bar to bar, StaffPad will convert your handwriting into a beautifully engraved score. You can draw notes, beams, stems, articulations, accidentals, slurs, ties and more. It’s the most natural way to write music on digital device, ever.\r\n\r\nAN ORCHESTRA IN THE TIP OF YOUR PEN\r\nStaffPad contains a bespoke playback engine, and an entire orchestra which has been meticulously recorded and programmed to play back your score with incredible realism. Everything from a basic piano lead sheet to a full symphony score can be written with StaffPad.\r\n\r\nA BEAUTIFUL EXPERIENCE\r\nWriting music should be the focus of a composer. StaffPad handles everything else for you whilst you work. Use your finger to move around the score, and pinch to zoom - with butter-smooth scrolling. When you want to write music, just use the pen. Use your eraser button on the pen to remove both ink strokes and existing notation. You can also draw freehand on the score, using the sketch layer, to quickly brainstorm and leave notes/comments for yourself and others.\r\n\r\nPRINT YOUR RESULTS\r\nStaffPad will intelligently layout the score when it’s time to print. You can print the entire score, as well as individual parts for each musician.
